# Dashboard Inventory — Master List v1.6.29

Source: `Master_List/Current Production Script/v.1.6.29_Current_Production_Script`.
Dashboard sheet: `Format Dashboard`. Cell addresses are the default generated locations from `writeDashboardDefaultsFast_()` with a 14-column dashboard width.
